### Post by What is in a name? on 2008-05-23
> **tw3k said:**
> how u get transparency in the menu?

I'm using Fluxbox; on the Configurations submenu, you have some options to set transparency levels on the menus and/or window titles. If you don't have a composite manager on like xcompmgr, you'll also need to enable pseudo-transparency on the same submenu.

### Post by urukrama on 2008-05-25
> **Istonian said:**
> How in the world did you get global-menu to work right? I have been trying forever.

I just followed the instructions on the [project's homepage]("http://code.google.com/p/gnome2-globalmenu/wiki/InstallingonUbuntu"). I had some issues with dependencies, but a * sudo apt-get -f install* solved that. Once it is installed, you right-click on a panel > Add to Panel and click on Global Menu.

### Post by Breakage on 2008-05-26
@el mariachi: No probs man, sure. I'm not currently using urxvt or xterm i'm using xfce terminal, so all the colours and tweaks can be done in terminal perferences and are saved to '~/.config/Terminal/terminalrc'. I find it a little quicker when im rethemeing the desktop, i'll up my terminal config so you can take a look. [[link]]("http://homepage.ntlworld.com/ashley.heron87/xfceterminal.tar.gz")

### Post by Breakage on 2008-05-26
> **What is in a name? said:**
> Though I believe some details like colouring your username might be somewhere on the .bashrc file, no? I always wanted to try out something on that sense myself. I'm giving a try to urxvt at the moment.

Yeah the username@hostname line is done in .bashrc,
you've gotta change the PS1= line here's mine. :)

But after the colours are set for the PS1= line they can be changed by the terminal.

> PS1='\[\e[0;33m\]\h\[\e[0;32m\]\w \[\e[0m\]\$ '

---

### Post by ayoli on 2008-05-26
> **Breakage said:**
> Yeah the username@hostname line is done in .bashrc,
you've gotta change the PS1= line here's mine. :)

But after the colours are set for the PS1= line they can be changed by the terminal.

There is [a thread]("http://ubuntuforums.org/showthread.php?t=679762&highlight=show+bashrc") plenty of bashrc confs.

Openbox themerc:

```

# based on Dyne

# To disable window decorations, add this to your ~/.config/openbox/rc.xml file
# under the applications section (around line 475):
#
#     <application class="*">
#      <decor>no</decor>
#     </application>
#

# Window geometry
padding.width: 1
border.width: 1
window.client.padding.width: 0
window.client.padding.height: 0
window.handle.width: 2

#Menu geometry
menu.border.width: 1
menu.overlap: -3

# Border colors
window.active.border.color: #000000
window.inactive.border.color: #eaeaea
menu.border.color: #000000
window.active.client.color: #eaeaea
window.inactive.client.color: #eaeaea

# Text shadows
window.active.label.text.font: shadow=n
window.inactive.label.text.font: shadow=n
menu.items.font: shadow=n
menu.title.text.font: shadow=n

# Window title justification
window.label.text.justify: left

# Active window
window.active.title.bg: Flat Solid
window.active.title.bg.color: #c0c0c0
window.active.label.bg: Parentrelative
window.active.label.text.color: #c0c0c0

window.active.handle.bg: Flat Solid
window.active.handle.bg.color: #eaeaea

window.active.grip.bg: Flat Gradient Vertical
window.active.grip.bg.color: #eaeaea
window.active.grip.bg.colorTo: #eaeaea

window.active.button.unpressed.bg: Parentrelative
window.active.button.pressed.bg: Parentrelative
window.active.button.disabled.bg: Parentrelative
window.active.button.toggled.bg: Parentrelative
window.active.button.hover.bg: Parentrelative

# Inactive windows
window.inactive.title.bg: Flat Gradient Vertical
window.inactive.title.bg.color: #000000
window.inactive.title.bg.colorTo: #000000

window.inactive.label.bg: Parentrelative
window.inactive.label.text.color: #000000

window.inactive.handle.bg: Flat Gradient Vertical
window.inactive.handle.bg.color: #eaeaea
window.inactive.handle.bg.colorTo: #eaeaea

window.inactive.grip.bg: Flat Gradient Vertical
window.inactive.grip.bg.color: #eaeaea
window.inactive.grip.bg.colorTo: #eaeaea

window.inactive.button.unpressed.bg: Flat Gradient Vertical Border
window.inactive.button.unpressed.bg.color: #000000
window.inactive.button.unpressed.bg.colorTo: #000000
window.inactive.button.unpressed.bg.border.color: #000000
window.inactive.button.unpressed.image.color: #000000

window.inactive.button.pressed.bg: Flat Gradient Vertical Border
window.inactive.button.pressed.bg.color: #000000
window.inactive.button.pressed.bg.colorTo: #000000
window.inactive.button.pressed.bg.border.color: #000000
window.inactive.button.pressed.image.color: #000000

window.inactive.button.disabled.bg: Flat Gradient Vertical Border
window.inactive.button.disabled.bg.color: #000000
window.inactive.button.disabled.bg.colorTo: #000000
window.inactive.button.disabled.bg.border.color: #000000
window.inactive.button.disabled.image.color: #000000

window.inactive.button.toggled.bg: Flat Gradient Vertical Border
window.inactive.button.toggled.bg.color: #000000
window.inactive.button.toggled.bg.colorTo: #000000
window.inactive.button.toggled.bg.border.color: #000000
window.inactive.button.toggled.image.color: #000000

window.inactive.button.hover.bg: Flat Gradient Vertical Border
window.inactive.button.hover.bg.color: #000000
window.inactive.button.hover.bg.colorTo: #000000
window.inactive.button.hover.bg.border.color: #000000
window.inactive.button.hover.image.color: #000000

# Menus
menu.title.bg: Flat Gradient Vertical
menu.title.bg.color: #222222
menu.title.bg.colorTo: #222222
menu.title.text.color: #c0c0c0
menu.title.text.justify: Left

menu.items.bg: Flat Solid
menu.items.bg.color: #000000
menu.items.text.color: #707070
menu.items.disabled.text.color: #c3c3c3

menu.items.active.bg: Flat Gradient Vertical
menu.items.active.bg.color: #000000
menu.items.active.bg.colorTo: #000000
menu.items.active.text.color: #ffffff
menu.items.active.disabled.text.color: #c3c3c3

#osd
osd.border.width: 1
osd.border.color:  #707070

osd.bg: flat border vertical gradient
osd.bg.color: #000000
osd.bg.colorTo: #000000
osd.bg.border.color: #000000

osd.label.bg: parentrelative

osd.label.text.color: #ffffff

```.conkyrc:
```

own_window no
own_window_hints undecorated,below,skip_taskbar,skip_pager
background no

double_buffer yes

use_spacer yes
use_xft yes

update_interval 3.0

minimum_size 100 20

draw_shades yes

draw_outline no
draw_borders no

uppercase no

stippled_borders 8

border_margin 4

border_width 1

default_color cccccc
default_shade_color 000000
default_outline_color 555555


own_window_colour 222222
own_window_transparent yes

alignment top_right

gap_x 10
gap_y 130


override_utf8_locale no
xftfont consolas:pixelsize=10
xftalpha 1.0

# ${color #3A3D42}${time %H:%M, %a %e %B}

TEXT
${color #ffffff}CPU ${color #ff8000}${cpubar 6,60}

    ${cpugraph 12,60 A985FF ff8000}

     ${color #3633FF}NAME                CPU%   MEM%
     ${color #e5e5e5}${top name 1}    ${top cpu 1} ${top mem 1}
     ${color #c4c4c4}${top name 2}    ${top cpu 2} ${top mem 2}
     ${color #a3a3a3}${top name 3}    ${top cpu 3} ${top mem 3}
     ${color #828282}${top name 4}    ${top cpu 4} ${top mem 4}

${color #ffffff}DSK ${color #ff8000}${fs_bar 6,60 /}

${color #ffffff}MEM ${color #ff8000}${membar 6,60}

     ${color #3633FF}NAME                CPU%   MEM%
     ${color #e5e5e5}${top_mem name 1}    ${top_mem cpu 1} ${top_mem mem 1}
     ${color #c4c4c4}${top_mem name 2}    ${top_mem cpu 2} ${top_mem mem 2}
     ${color #a3a3a3}${top_mem name 3}    ${top_mem cpu 3} ${top_mem mem 3}
     ${color #828282}${top_mem name 4}    ${top_mem cpu 4} ${top_mem mem 4}

${color #ffffff}MSG  ${color #ff8000}${execi 100 sh ~/.config/scripts/gmail.sh}

${color #ffffff}NET ${color #ff8000}${upspeedgraph eth1 12,60 A985FFni9ce ff8000}

    ${color #ff8000}${downspeedgraph eth1 12,60 A985FF ff8000}

${color #ffffff}SWP ${color #ff8000}${swapbar 6,60}

```gmail.sh:
```

#!/bin/bash

gmail_login=" "  
gmail_password=" " 

dane="$(wget --secure-protocol=TLSv1 --timeout=3 -t 1 -q -O - \
https://${gmail_login}:${gmail_password}@mail.google.com/mail/feed/atom \
--no-check-certificate | grep 'fullcount' \
| sed -e 's/.*<fullcount>//;s/<\/fullcount>.*//' 2>/dev/null)"

if [ -z "$dane" ]; then
echo "! "
else
echo "$dane Unread"
fi
